    validator.fix(chapter)

# ❌ Role matching
if section.role == slot.role:
    ...

# ❌ Variable section counts

    add_more_sections()

# ❌ Dynamic selection
selected = select_from_pool(slot.role)

# ❌ Cross-slot substitution

    use_slot_02_content()

### ✅ Required Patterns

python
# ✅ Fixed iteration
for slot in sorted(chapter_template.slots, key=lambda s: s.position):
    ...

# ✅ Deterministic selection
variant_idx = choose_variant(slot_id, chapter_id, seed)

# ✅ Hard abort
if variant_idx < 0 or variant_idx >= 5:
    raise SlotAssemblyError(...)

# ✅ Direct rendering
content = render_slot_content(slot_id, variant, chapter_id)

# ✅ Fixed count check
if len(chapter_template.slots) != 10:
    raise SlotAssemblyError("Must have exactly 10 slots")

## Code Complexity Check

### Real Slot Assembler

- **Lines of code:** ~150-200 (core algorithm)
- **Functions:** 3-4 (assemble, choose_variant, render_slot_content)
- **Conditionals:** Minimal (error checks only)
- **Loops:** 1 (iterate 10 slots)
- **External calls:** SectionLoader.load_section() only

### Fake Slot Assembler

- **Lines of code:** 500+ (trying to handle all cases)
- **Functions:** 10+ (selection, filtering, fallback, recovery)
- **Conditionals:** Many (if/else for different scenarios)
- **Loops:** Multiple (iterating pools, filtering candidates)
- **External calls:** Validator, pool manager, fallback handler

**Rule of thumb:** If the assembler is >300 lines, it's probably doing too much.

---

## Function Call Graph

### Real Slot Assembler

assemble_chapter_slots()
  ├─ sorted(chapter_template.slots)  # Sort by position
  ├─ choose_variant()                 # Deterministic selection
  ├─ render_slot_content()           # Load and render
  └─ raise SlotAssemblyError()       # If anything fails

**Depth:** 2-3 levels  
**Branches:** 1 (the loop)  
**External dependencies:** SectionLoader only

### Fake Slot Assembler

assemble_chapter_slots()
  ├─ get_available_sections()        # ❌ Pool access
  ├─ filter_by_role()                # ❌ Role matching
  ├─ select_from_pool()              # ❌ Pool selection
  ├─ validator.check()               # ❌ Validation
  ├─ fallback_handler()              # ❌ Fallback
  └─ recovery_logic()                # ❌ Recovery

**Depth:** 5+ levels  
**Branches:** Many (if/else for different cases)  
**External dependencies:** Pool manager, validator, fallback handler

## Test Coverage Check

def test_exactly_10_slots():
    """Verify exactly 10 slots per chapter."""
    result = assemble_chapter_slots(...)
    assert len(result.slots) == 10

def test_variant_index_range():
    """Verify variant_index is 0-4."""
    for slot in result.slots:
        assert 0 <= slot.variant_index < 5

def test_determinism():
    """Verify same inputs → same outputs."""
    result1 = assemble_chapter_slots(seed=12345, ...)
    result2 = assemble_chapter_slots(seed=12345, ...)
    assert result1.slots == result2.slots

def test_hard_abort():
    """Verify missing variant → SlotAssemblyError."""
    with pytest.raises(SlotAssemblyError):
        assemble_chapter_slots(missing_variant=True, ...)

## Review Checklist

When reviewing the PR, check:

- [ ] Assembler is <300 lines (core algorithm)
- [ ] Only 1 loop (iterate 10 slots)
- [ ] No pool access code
- [ ] No fallback logic
- [ ] No validator calls in assembly path
- [ ] choose_variant() is deterministic (hash-based)
- [ ] Hard abort on any failure (no try/except that continues)
- [ ] Fixed slot count check (exactly 10)
- [ ] Variant index range check (0-4)
- [ ] Tests are simple (4-6 tests, not 10+)

**If ANY checkbox fails → PR rejected.**

      "chapter": 1,
      "slots": [
        {"slot": "slot_01_open", "variant": "v2", "variant_index": 1},
        {"slot": "slot_02_scene", "variant": "v4", "variant_index": 3},
        {"slot": "slot_03_context", "variant": "v1", "variant_index": 0},
        {"slot": "slot_04_reflection", "variant": "v3", "variant_index": 2},
        {"slot": "slot_05_reframe", "variant": "v5", "variant_index": 4},
        {"slot": "slot_06_practice_intro", "variant": "v1", "variant_index": 0},
        {"slot": "slot_07_practice", "variant": "v2", "variant_index": 1},
        {"slot": "slot_08_integration", "variant": "v4", "variant_index": 3},
        {"slot": "slot_09_closure", "variant": "v3", "variant_index": 2},
        {"slot": "slot_10_takeaway", "variant": "v1", "variant_index": 0}
      ]
    },
    {
      "chapter": 2,
      "slots": [
        {"slot": "slot_01_open", "variant": "v3", "variant_index": 2},
        ...
      ]
    },
    ...
  ]
}

### Key Characteristics

1. ✅ **Exactly 10 slots per chapter** (no more, no less)
2. ✅ **Fixed slot IDs:** slot_01_open → slot_10_takeaway
3. ✅ **Variant format:** v1, v2, v3, v4, v5 (not scene_f3 or hook_variant_2)
4. ✅ **Variant index:** 0-4 (matches variant: v1=0, v2=1, v3=2, v4=3, v5=4)
5. ✅ **Same slot IDs across chapters:** Every chapter has slot_01_open, slot_02_scene, etc.
6. ✅ **Deterministic:** Same seed → same variant selections

---

## ❌ Fake Compliance Patterns

Reject immediately if you see **any** of these:

### Pattern 1: Section IDs Instead of Slot IDs

json
{
  "chapter": 1,
  "sections": [
    {"section": "ch01_sec01", "variant": "f1"},
    {"section": "ch01_sec03", "variant": "f2"},
    ...
  ]
}

**Why it's fake:**
- Uses ch01_secXX format (section IDs, not slot IDs)
- Variable count (not exactly 10)
- Section IDs don't map to fixed slots

**Rejection reason:** "Section IDs indicate pool-based selection, not slot-based assembly."

---

### Pattern 2: Variable Slot Counts

json
{
  "chapter": 1,
  "slots": [
    {"slot": "slot_01_open", "variant": "v2"},
    {"slot": "slot_02_scene", "variant": "v1"},
    {"slot": "slot_03_context", "variant": "v3"}
    // Only 3 slots!
  ]
}

**Why it's fake:**
- Not exactly 10 slots
- Missing slots 4-10

**Rejection reason:** "Chapter must have exactly 10 slots. Found {count}."

---

### Pattern 3: Reused Section IDs Across Chapters

json
{
  "chapters": [
    {
      "chapter": 1,
      "slots": [
        {"slot": "ch01_sec03", "variant": "f1"},
        ...
      ]
    },
    {
      "chapter": 5,
      "slots": [
        {"slot": "ch01_sec03", "variant": "f2"},  // ❌ Same section ID!
        ...
      ]
    }
  ]
}

**Why it's fake:**
- Section IDs like ch01_sec03 reused across chapters
- Indicates shared pool, not chapter-specific slots

**Rejection reason:** "Section IDs reused across chapters indicates pool-based selection."

---

### Pattern 4: Missing Slot Numbers

json
{
  "chapter": 1,
  "slots": [
    {"slot": "slot_01_open", "variant": "v2"},
    {"slot": "slot_02_scene", "variant": "v1"},
    {"slot": "slot_05_reframe", "variant": "v3"},  // ❌ Skipped 3 and 4!
    ...
  ]
}

**Why it's fake:**
- Missing slots 3 and 4
- Not sequential 1-10

**Rejection reason:** "Slots must be sequential 1-10. Missing slots: {list}."

---

### Pattern 5: Non-Standard Variant Names

json
{
  "chapter": 1,
  "slots": [
    {"slot": "slot_01_open", "variant": "scene_f3"},  // ❌ Not v1-v5!
    {"slot": "slot_02_scene", "variant": "hook_variant_2"},
    ...
  ]
}

**Why it's fake:**
- Variant names don't match v1, v2, v3, v4, v5
- Indicates role-based selection, not slot-based

**Rejection reason:** "Variants must be v1-v5. Found: {variant_names}."

---

### Pattern 6: "Selected From" or "Resolved Via" Metadata

json
{
  "chapter": 1,
  "slots": [
    {
      "slot": "slot_01_open",
      "variant": "v2",
      "selected_from": "hook_pool",  // ❌ Pool reference!
      "resolved_via": "role_match"
    }
  ]
}

**Why it's fake:**
- Metadata indicates pool selection
- "Resolved via role match" = pool-based

**Rejection reason:** "Metadata indicates pool-based selection, not slot-based assembly."

---

### Pattern 7: Different Slot IDs Per Chapter

json
{
  "chapters": [
    {
      "chapter": 1,
      "slots": [
        {"slot": "slot_01_open", "variant": "v2"},
        {"slot": "slot_02_scene", "variant": "v1"},
        ...
      ]
    },
    {
      "chapter": 2,
      "slots": [
        {"slot": "slot_01_context", "variant": "v3"},  // ❌ Different slot name!
        {"slot": "slot_02_reflection", "variant": "v1"},
        ...
      ]
    }
  ]
}

**Why it's fake:**
- Slot IDs differ across chapters
- Indicates dynamic selection, not fixed slots

**Rejection reason:** "Slot IDs must be identical across chapters. Found different IDs."

---

### Pattern 8: Non-Deterministic Variants

json
{
  "chapters": [
    {
      "chapter": 1,
      "slots": [
        {"slot": "slot_01_open", "variant": "v2"},
        ...
      ]
    }
  ]
}

**Then run again with same seed:**

json
{
  "chapters": [
    {
      "chapter": 1,
      "slots": [
        {"slot": "slot_01_open", "variant": "v4"},  // ❌ Different variant!
        ...
      ]
    }
  ]
}

**Why it's fake:**
- Same seed → different variant selections
- Indicates randomness or heuristics, not deterministic selection

**Rejection reason:** "Variant selection is not deterministic. Same seed produced different selections."

---

## Quick Check Script

python
import json
from pathlib import Path

def check_slot_assembly_artifact(debug_json_path: Path) -> tuple[bool, list[str]]:
    """
    Check if chapter_slots_debug.json indicates real slot-based assembly.
    
    Returns:
        (is_valid, error_messages)
    """
    errors = []
    
    with open(debug_json_path) as f:
        data = json.load(f)
    
    # Check structure
    if "chapters" not in data:
        return False, ["Missing 'chapters' key"]
    
    chapters = data["chapters"]
    
    # Check chapter count
    if len(chapters) != 12:
        errors.append(f"Expected 12 chapters, got {len(chapters)}")
    
    # Check each chapter
    for chapter_data in chapters:
        chapter_num = chapter_data.get("chapter")
        slots = chapter_data.get("slots", [])
        
        # Check slot count
        if len(slots) != 10:
            errors.append(
                f"Chapter {chapter_num}: Expected 10 slots, got {len(slots)}"
            )
        
        # Check slot IDs
        expected_slot_ids = [
            f"slot_{i:02d}_{name}"
            for i, name in enumerate([
                "open", "scene", "context", "reflection", "reframe",
                "practice_intro", "practice", "integration", "closure", "takeaway"
            ], 1)
        ]
        
        actual_slot_ids = [s.get("slot") for s in slots]
        
        if set(actual_slot_ids) != set(expected_slot_ids):
            errors.append(
                f"Chapter {chapter_num}: Slot IDs don't match expected. "
                f"Expected: {expected_slot_ids}, Got: {actual_slot_ids}"
            )
        
        # Check variant format
        for slot in slots:
            variant = slot.get("variant", "")
            if not variant.startswith("v") or variant not in ["v1", "v2", "v3", "v4", "v5"]:
                errors.append(
                    f"Chapter {chapter_num}, {slot.get('slot')}: "
                    f"Invalid variant format: {variant}. Must be v1-v5."
                )
    
    return len(errors) == 0, errors

# Usage
debug_path = Path("output_books/qa_book_*/chapter_slots_debug.json")
is_valid, errors = check_slot_assembly_artifact(debug_path)

if not is_valid:
    print("❌ REJECTED: Fake compliance detected")
    for error in errors:
        print(f"  - {error}")
else:
    print("✅ ACCEPTED: Real slot-based assembly")

    ├─ NO → REJECT (wrong chapter count)

        ├─ NO → REJECT (wrong slot count)
        └─ YES → Are slot IDs slot_01_open → slot_10_takeaway?
            ├─ NO → REJECT (wrong slot IDs)
            └─ YES → Are variants v1-v5?
                ├─ NO → REJECT (wrong variant format)
                └─ YES → Is selection deterministic?
                    ├─ NO → REJECT (non-deterministic)
                    └─ YES → ACCEPT (real slot-based assembly)

## Step 2: Quick Code Scan (5 Minutes)

### Open slot_assembler.py

**Look for:**

1. **Function count**
   - Should be 3-4 functions (assemble, choose_variant, render_slot_content)
   - If 10+ functions → red flag

2. **Line count**
   - Should be ~150-200 lines (core algorithm)
   - If 500+ lines → red flag

3. **Banned keywords** (Ctrl+F)
   - pool → red flag
   - fallback → red flag
   - substitute → red flag
   - recovery → red flag
   - validator → red flag (in assembly path)

4. **Loop count**
   - Should be 1 loop (iterate 10 slots)
   - If multiple loops → red flag

### If Red Flags Found

- **Stop review**
- **Reject immediately**
- **Reason:** "Code contains banned patterns. See SLOT_ASSEMBLER_SANITY_CHECK.md."

## General Mapping Pattern

### Slot Mapping Rules

1. **HOOK sections** → slot_01_open
2. **SCENE sections** → slot_02_scene
3. **First REFLECTION** → slot_03_context or slot_04_reflection
4. **Subsequent REFLECTIONS** → slot_04_reflection, slot_05_reframe, or slot_08_integration
5. **INTEGRATION sections** → slot_08_integration or slot_09_closure
6. **NEW slots** → slot_06_practice_intro, slot_07_practice, slot_10_takeaway

### Variant Mapping

**From Intake Files:**
- F1 → v1
- F2 → v2
- F3 → v3
- F4 → v4
- F5 → v5

**If only 1 variant exists:**
- Use as v1
- Create v2, v3, v4, v5 as variations

---

## Content Creation Strategy

### Phase 1: Use Existing Variants

For sections that already have 5 variants (like Chapter 5 Section 01 and 02):
- Copy content directly
- Map F1-F5 → v1-v5
- Verify uniqueness

### Phase 2: Expand Single Variants

For sections with only 1 variant:
- Use existing as v1
- Create v2-v5 as distinct variations
- Maintain same purpose/type
- Ensure uniqueness

### Phase 3: Create New Slots

For slots that don't exist in intake files:
- slot_06_practice_intro - Create all 5 variants
- slot_07_practice - Create all 5 variants (or prose-only if no exercise)
- slot_10_takeaway - Create all 5 variants

## Quick Reference: Intake File Structure

Each intake file (CHAPTER_{NN}_V3_FINAL.md) contains:

1. **Section Map Table** - Lists all sections with types and variant counts
2. **Variant Family Coverage Table** - Shows which sections have F1-F5
3. **Section Content** - Full prose for each variant

**Key Sections to Check:**
- Section 01 (HOOK) - Usually has 5 variants
- Section 02 (SCENE) - Usually has 5 variants
- Sections 03+ (REFLECTION/INTEGRATION) - Usually have 1 variant

---

## Content Team Instructions

1. **Read intake file** for each chapter (intake_chps/CHAPTER_{NN}_V3_FINAL.md)

2. **Map sections to slots** using the pattern above

3. **For slots with 5 variants:**
   - Copy content directly (F1→v1, F2→v2, etc.)
   - Verify uniqueness

4. **For slots with 1 variant:**
   - Use existing as v1
   - Create 4 new variants (v2-v5) with distinct approaches

5. **For new slots:**
   - Create all 5 variants from scratch
   - Follow slot purpose guidelines

6. **Create YAML files** in structure:
   
chapter_{NN}/slot_{XX}_{name}/v{N}.yaml

## ❗ Read This First

## ✅ Your Job (In One Sentence)

For **each chapter**, write **10 slots × 5 variants = 50 pieces of prose**, where each variant is a different expression of the *same moment or idea*, written fully (no placeholders).

---

## 🧱 Canonical Slots (Do Not Change These)

Every chapter has **exactly these 10 slots**:

1. slot_01_open — opening recognition / hook
2. slot_02_scene — concrete lived moment (scene)
3. slot_03_context — what's actually happening / pattern exposure
4. slot_04_reflection — emotional recognition
5. slot_05_reframe — meaning shift / insight
6. slot_06_practice_intro — introduce the practice (why it helps)
7. slot_07_practice — the practice itself (or embodied instruction)
8. slot_08_integration — connect insight + action
9. slot_09_closure — emotional closure
10. slot_10_takeaway — final takeaway / memory anchor

These slots are **fixed**.
Do not rename, reorder, merge, or invent new ones.

---

## 🎭 Variants (Required)

Each slot must have **exactly 5 variants**:

* v1 — direct / plain
* v2 — peer / conversational
* v3 — poetic / image-driven
* v4 — coach / guiding
* v5 — somatic / body-aware

**Important:** These style labels are **writer guidance** to help you create distinct variants. The system doesn't enforce these specific styles—it only requires that:
- All 5 variants exist
- They are distinct from each other
- They express the same core idea
- They match the slot's purpose

All 5 variants must:

* Express the **same core idea**
* Be meaning-equivalent
* Feel genuinely different in voice and texture

---

## 🎬 Where Scene Content Goes (Important)

**Scenes are not separate files.**

* No scene_XX.yaml
* No {scene_XX} placeholders
* No scene objects

Instead:

* Concrete lived moments (e.g. *Verve coffee*, *Seabright bonfire*)
  are written **directly inside the variants**, usually in:

  * slot_02_scene
  * sometimes slot_03_context or slot_04_reflection

Example:

* The *same* Verve coffee moment is written **5 different ways** in
  slot_02_scene_v1 → slot_02_scene_v5

---

## ❌ What Not To Do

* ❌ Do not invent "sections"
* ❌ Do not decide slot order
* ❌ Do not leave slots empty
* ❌ Do not write fewer than 5 variants
* ❌ Do not reference other slots ("as mentioned above")
* ❌ Do not assume the reader saw another variant

Each variant must stand alone.

---

## 📁 File Structure

### Directory Layout

phoenix_v4/libraries/sections/
├── chapter_01/
│   ├── slot_01_open/
│   │   ├── v1.yaml
│   │   ├── v2.yaml

│   │   └── v5.yaml

│   │   ├── v1.yaml

│   │   └── ... (5 variants)

### File Naming Convention

**Format:** {chapter_id}/slot_{position:02d}_{slot_name}/v{variant_num}.yaml

**Examples:**
- chapter_01/slot_01_open/v1.yaml
- chapter_01/slot_01_open/v2.yaml
- chapter_01/slot_02_scene/v1.yaml
- chapter_05/slot_07_practice/v3.yaml
- chapter_12/slot_10_takeaway/v5.yaml

## 📄 YAML File Format

Each variant file (v1.yaml through v5.yaml) must follow this structure:

yaml
variant_id: ch01_slot_01_open_v1
chapter: 1
section: 1
section_type: hook
purpose: opening
variant_family: v1
content: |
  [The actual prose content goes here.
  
  This is the text that will appear in the book.
  
  It should be complete, coherent prose that fits the slot's purpose.]
fingerprint:
  word_count: 150
  paragraph_count: 3
  has_dialogue: false
  has_scene: true
metadata:
  duration: standard
  style: narrative
  tone: recognition

### Required Fields

- **variant_id**: Must match file path (ch{chapter:02d}_slot_{position:02d}_{slot_name}_v{variant_num})
  - Example: ch01_slot_01_open_v1 for chapter_01/slot_01_open/v1.yaml
- **chapter**: Chapter number (1-12)
- **section**: Slot position (1-10)
- **section_type**: Slot type (hook, scene, reflection, exercise, integration)
  - Map: slot_01_open → hook, slot_02_scene → scene, slot_07_practice → exercise, etc.
- **purpose**: Slot purpose (matches slot description)
  - Example: "opening", "situational grounding", "pattern exposure", etc.
- **variant_family**: Variant identifier (v1, v2, v3, v4, v5)
- **content**: The actual prose text (required, cannot be empty)
  - This is the text that appears in the book
  - Must be complete, coherent prose
  - No placeholders or fragments
- **fingerprint**: Metadata about the content
  - word_count: Approximate word count
  - paragraph_count: Number of paragraphs
  - has_dialogue: true/false
  - has_scene: true/false
- **metadata**: Additional metadata
  - duration: standard (or short/long if applicable)
  - style: narrative, instructional, etc.
  - tone: recognition, reflection, etc.

  I stood outside the Verve coffee shop, cup cooling in my hands, watching people rush past while I waited again. The steam had stopped rising minutes ago, but I couldn't bring myself to go inside.   The street was full of motion—people with places to be, conversations to have, lives that seemed to move forward without hesitation. And there I was, frozen, holding a cup of coffee that was no longer warm, trying to find the right words for a moment that had already passed.

## 🧠 How to Work (Recommended Process)

1. Read the intake chapter (CHAPTER_XX_V3_FINAL.md)
2. Identify which **ideas map to which slots**
3. For each slot:

   * Decide the core message
   * Write 5 stylistic variants of that same message
   * Create 5 YAML files (v1.yaml through v5.yaml)
4. Move to the next slot
5. Do **not** think about flow across slots — the system handles order

---

## ✅ Final Mental Model

> **You are not writing a chapter.**
> **You are writing 10 reusable moments, each expressed 5 ways.**

If you do that, the system works perfectly.

---

## 📋 Content Requirements

### 1. Uniqueness Within Slot

**All 5 variants for the same slot must be distinct.**

- ch01_slot_01_open_v1 ≠ ch01_slot_01_open_v2 ≠ v3 ≠ v4 ≠ v5
- No duplicate content within a slot
- Each variant should offer a different approach/angle

### 2. Consistency Across Chapters

**Same slot position can reuse similar approaches across chapters.**

- ch01_slot_01_open_v1 and ch05_slot_01_open_v1 can be similar
- But ch01_slot_01_open_v1 and ch01_slot_01_open_v2 must be distinct

### 3. Slot Purpose Alignment

**Content must match the slot's purpose.**

- slot_01_open → Opening/recognition content
- slot_02_scene → Scene/situational content
- slot_05_reframe → Reframing/insight content
- etc.

### 4. Prose Quality

**Content must be:**
- Complete prose (not fragments)
- Coherent and readable
- Therapeutically appropriate
- Persona/topic appropriate (when applicable)

# After parsing variant_id for slot format:
if slot_match:
    # Try slot-based structure first
    slot_file = (
        self.sections_root /
        f"chapter_{chapter_num:02d}" /
        f"slot_{slot_pos:02d}_{slot_name}" /
        f"v{variant_num}.yaml"
    )

        variant_file = slot_file

        variant_file = (

            f"chapter_{chapter_num:02d}" /
            f"section_{section_num:02d}_{section_type.lower()}" /
            f"{variant_family.lower()}.yaml"
        )

✅ 1. Content Completeness Validator (600 / 600)
Goal
Fail before generation if any slot variant is missing.

What to Validate
Per chapter:
10 slots
5 variants each
Exactly 50 files
Global:
12 chapters
Exactly 600 files

Validator Logic (Authoritative)
Create:


phoenix_v4/validator/content_completeness_validator.py

Minimal, explicit implementation


from pathlib import Path

EXPECTED_SLOTS = [
    "slot_01_open",
    "slot_02_scene",
    "slot_03_context",
    "slot_04_reflection",
    "slot_05_reframe",
    "slot_06_practice_intro",
    "slot_07_practice",
    "slot_08_integration",
    "slot_09_closure",
    "slot_10_takeaway",
]

EXPECTED_VARIANTS = ["v1.yaml", "v2.yaml", "v3.yaml", "v4.yaml", "v5.yaml"]

class ContentCompletenessError(Exception):
    pass


def validate_slot_content(sections_root: Path):
    errors = []
    total_files = 0

    for chapter in range(1, 13):
        chapter_dir = sections_root / f"chapter_{chapter:02d}"

        if not chapter_dir.exists():
            errors.append(f"Missing chapter directory: chapter_{chapter:02d}")
            continue

        for slot in EXPECTED_SLOTS:
            slot_dir = chapter_dir / slot

            if not slot_dir.exists():
                errors.append(f"Missing slot dir: chapter_{chapter:02d}/{slot}")
                continue

            for variant in EXPECTED_VARIANTS:
                variant_path = slot_dir / variant
                if not variant_path.exists():
                    errors.append(
                        f"Missing variant: chapter_{chapter:02d}/{slot}/{variant}"
                    )
                else:
                    total_files += 1

    if errors:
        raise ContentCompletenessError(
            "Content completeness check failed:\n" + "\n".join(errors)
        )

    if total_files != 600:
        raise ContentCompletenessError(
            f"Expected 600 content files, found {total_files}"
        )

    return True


Where to Call It (Hard Gate)
Call this before any book generation:


validate_slot_content(
    Path("phoenix_v4/libraries/sections")
)

If it fails → abort immediately.
No fallback. No warnings.

Optional Test (Recommended)


phoenix_v4/tests/test_content_completeness.py



def test_content_completeness():
    from pathlib import Path
    from phoenix_v4.validator.content_completeness_validator import validate_slot_content

    assert validate_slot_content(
        Path("phoenix_v4/libraries/sections")
    ) is True

📐 SPEC: Story Quota Tuning (Correct-Failure Resolution)
Scope: Planning layer only Non-Goals: No assembly changes, no injector changes, no content changes Principle: Failures stay real; defaults become sane per format

1️⃣ Problem Statement (Precise)
The system currently correctly fails when:
The planner assigns too many stories per chapter
The format quota allows fewer stories
Example (from your demo):
Medium book → planner emits 2 stories/chapter
Format quota → allows 1
Result → hard failure
This is architecturally correct, but operationally noisy during demos and default runs.

2️⃣ Core Invariant (DO NOT VIOLATE)
Quotas are enforced. The system must never silently drop stories. Failures must remain failures when limits are exceeded.
We are not weakening enforcement. We are aligning planner defaults with format intent.

3️⃣ Correct Fix Location
✅ ONLY in the planning layer ❌ Not in assembler ❌ Not in injector ❌ Not in validator ❌ Not in quotas themselves
Specifically:


phoenix_v4/planning/story_plan_v2.py
phoenix_v4/planning/format_blueprints.yaml


4️⃣ New Responsibility Split
Before (Problematic)
Planner decides story count
Format enforces quota
Mismatch causes frequent failures
After (Correct)
Format declares max stories
Planner reads that limit
Planner emits ≤ quota by default
Validator still enforces hard cap

5️⃣ Format-Level Story Quota Spec (Authoritative)
Add or confirm this field in every format blueprint:


story_quota:
  per_chapter:
    min: 0
    max: 1

Recommended Defaults (MVP)
Format
Stories / Chapter
Rationale
standard_book_long
max: 2
Deep narrative allowed
standard_book_medium
max: 1
Avoid overload
standard_book_short
max: 0
Recognition-first
seven_day_reset
max: 0–1
Light grounding only
pocket_guide
max: 0
Zero narrative
podcast
max: 1
Spoken anchor only
practice_anthology
max: 0
No stories
Key: Formats decide narrative density — not the planner.

6️⃣ Planner Behavior Change (Exact)
Old (Implicit / Hardcoded)


stories_per_chapter = 2

New (Format-Aware)


max_allowed = format_blueprint.story_quota.per_chapter.max
stories_per_chapter = min(DEFAULT_STORY_TARGET, max_allowed)

Where:


DEFAULT_STORY_TARGET = 2  # unchanged global preference


7️⃣ Validation Rules (Unchanged)
DO NOT CHANGE THESE
If planner emits > quota → ❌ error
If required story role missing → ❌ error
If injector cannot place story → ❌ error
Failures remain loud.

8️⃣ Why This Is the Correct Fix

✅ Determinism ✅ Honesty (no silent drops) ✅ Format authority ✅ Planning intelligence ✅ Clear failure modes
But eliminates:
demo noise
“false negative” runs
confusion during Phase 2.1 work
